FreeBSD Ports: X11-clocks
=========================

Search ports for: All Package Name Description Long description
Maintainer Requires

--------------

Uhren f?r das X Window-System.
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

**\ `abclock-1.0d\_3 <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/x11-clocks/abclock>`__**
    | Clock for X that displays hours and minutes in an analog fashion
    | `Long
      description <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/x11-clocks/abclock/pkg-descr?revision=HEAD>`__
      \|
      `Changes <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/x11-clocks/abclock/?view=log>`__
      \| `Main Web Site <http://odur.let.rug.nl/~kleiweg/abclock/>`__
    | *Maintained by:* ports@FreeBSD.org
    | *Requires:* `kbproto-1.0.6 <x11.html#kbproto-1.0.6>`__,
      `libX11-1.6.2\_3,1 <x11.html#libX11-1.6.2_3,1>`__,
      `libXau-1.0.8\_3 <x11.html#libXau-1.0.8_3>`__,
      `libXdmcp-1.1.2 <x11.html#libXdmcp-1.1.2>`__,
      `libpthread-stubs-0.3\_6 <devel.html#libpthread-stubs-0.3_6>`__,
      `libxcb-1.11\_1 <x11.html#libxcb-1.11_1>`__,
      `libxml2-2.9.2\_3 <textproc.html#libxml2-2.9.2_3>`__,
      `xproto-7.0.27 <x11.html#xproto-7.0.27>`__
